I've been pretending I wasn't not a perfume snob...but it seems I am...or was. <br />
<br />
I knew big brands might overcharge, but I thought it was justified. The artistry and creation certainly justifies prices but don't brands use better ingredients? Apparently not. <br />
<br />
The key is: I really thought the smell was superior in TF and other brands! Even when comparing brands side-by-side to clones, I'd persuade myself the brands smelt superior. I was wrong. <br />
<br />
This Rasasi is better, smoother and sexier than Tom Ford's TL - and TL was my signature for years! Gone is the acrid opening than I persuaded myself was cool, cocaine-like, manly and intense. More raspberry, more suede, more saffron, more balance! In fact, it smells better at the opening and more similar throughout the progression. That's a very good thing. <br />
<br />
I've  come to a similar realisation with Aventus and CDNIM(P), which isn't necessarily better but it's soooo similar I don't care.) I'm so glad I'll be saving money. 🙌🏻😊</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="19668"comment_id="2272250"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Rasasi/La-Yuqawam-Homme-19668.html?ccid=2272250#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,245,242,0.9); padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc2161582" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="WesFragrance"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/2139143"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.2139143.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="WesFragrance" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma2161582ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck3x2"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd2161582" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(250,247,236,0.87); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/2139143">WesFragrance</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-05-19">05/19/24 22:56</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>I recently sprayed Tom Ford Tuscan Leather and found it's scent profile addictive. La Yuqawam is my first clone purchase and it does not disappoint. The scent profiles are very similar, as others have said, there is a hint more of a raspberry note, it's slightly sweeter but the general profile is very similar to Tuscan Leather. <br />
<br />
I'm a huge fan of Tom Ford Oud Wood and own a bottle, it's one of my all time favourites. Disappointingly the performance is terrible for the price hence why I was reluctant to drop $500 on Tom Ford Tuscan Leather. With La Yuqawam I feel like I'm getting the Tom Ford experience for a fraction of the cost. If you want Tuscan Leather but don't want to spend the money then I recommend La Yuqawam as an alternative.<br />
<br />
Performance wise, I sprayed it two hours ago and it's holding up strong so far. It's not a beast like Mancera Red Tobacco but at the very least it's on par with Tom Ford Oud Wood during the initial two hours I've been wearing it.<br />
<br />
Batch date on the box was April 2022<br />
<br />
*Update<br />
<br />
I've worn this a few more times and can confirm the performance is excellent. It lasts on my skin and clothes all day. While the projection is moderate the longevity is very good. I went back to Mecca and did another direct side-by-side comparison with TF Tuscan Leather. There is a little more depth to the TF fragrance but once the dry down is complete it's very hard to tell any difference. I had a shower with both fragrances on, after the shower I couldn't smell Tuscan Leather but I could still smell La Yuqawam on my skin, the performance is very good overall.<br />
<br />
Final score 8.4/10</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="19668"comment_id="2161582"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Rasasi/La-Yuqawam-Homme-19668.html?ccid=2161582#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2145056" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,245,242,0.78);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:1,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:5,&quot;sillage&quot;:3,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;male&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc2057113" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="Israel26"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1508801"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.1508801.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="Israel26" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma2057113ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck3x3"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd2057113" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(249,249,243,0.81); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1508801">Israel26</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-02-09">02/09/24 07:36</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>Went through a full bottle of this. My most worn fragrance of 2023. I never get compliments on fragrances and don't really care for them but I got told I smell good by my closest friend and a stranger told me I stink. Sweet raspberries mixed with a slight bitter smell, leather, suede, low hints of gasoline and it remains this way but gets really woody at the dry down. On skin this lasts all day and I've had times where it lasts until the next day on skin and still survives the shower so you get a faint smell but still there.. on clothing it's a different story 24+ hours easy also I've had sweaters last up to weeks sitting in the closet no joke. This is definitely a powerful fragrance that will captivate peoples mind in a good way or a bad way so beware. Solid 9 for me.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="19668"comment_id="2057113"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Rasasi/La-Yuqawam-Homme-19668.html?ccid=2057113#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2040045" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,245,242,0.71);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:1,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:4,&quot;sillage&quot;:2,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;male&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc2040045" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="pejatibia"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1707864"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.1707864.gif" class="comments-avatar"alt="pejatibia" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"><span class="idLinkify" title="/perfume/Van-Cleef-Arpels/Midnight-in-Paris-9685.html"><img loading="lazy" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/perfume/mm.9685.jpg"class="perfume-wearing-icon" alt="Midnight in Paris"title="Midnight in Paris"></span></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma2040045ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck4x2"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd2040045" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(250,245,242,0.71); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1707864">pejatibia</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-01-23">01/23/24 18:35</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>Soundtrack for the review. Necessary to read the review properly. Playing it at least once while reading my review is a must; it's just got the same energy as this fragrance has:<br />
https://youtu.be/2qga9QLAaZ4<br />
<br />
La Yuqawam opens with a dramatically vivid and luxuriously textured velvet-lined raspberry smell that immediately greets you. As we venture deeper to the middle, the heart is predominantly based around artemisia, which I can clearly identify due to its herbal attributes.<br />
<br />
Moving towards the base, a smooth blend of woody suede emerges, which, despite the earlier changes, still projects decently, when you might be thinking it's the end, defying expectations of a swift fade. In terms of projection, it doesn’t quite live up to the 'beast' level that some claim. It's super strong at first and despite the complex metamorphosis, quickly dies down compared to how loud it was in the beginning. It still projects, but not as much, gracefully becoming a subtle, intimate presence.<br />
<br />
The longevity, however, is impressively transforming without losing its narrative thread. Reliable and steadfast through each phase of the fragrance's evolution, remaining consistent and engaging through each evolutionary phase.<br />
<br />
I can’t stop thinking about a comment I read which said, 'it smells like those rubber Halloween masks'. I spent a few hours sniffing it on and off my body to write this (just like any other review). After reading that comment, I had a huge nostalgia flashback for about 2 seconds, remembering when I wore such a mask at around 7 or 8 years old. When I freshly sprayed the fragrance again, especially the opening for the first 10 minutes, it smelled PRECISELY like those masks. It’s amazing what subtleties you can catch; congrats, man. A perfect nose. You found the hidden funky rubber scent.<br />
<br />
Nonetheless, this doesn’t change my opinion about the fragrance; I still think it's great. I love these kinds of quirks in fragrances. Far from altering my perception, they only deepen my appreciation for each fragrance's unique character.<br />
<br />
This is a very classy men’s fragrance. If you want to try something similar with a combination of raspberry and leather, I’d recommend Italian Leather by Just Jack. It is and smells slightly cheaper than La Yuqawam but it's still spot on. While slightly less opulent, it echoes the same refined blend of fruity suede.<br />
<br />
By the way, finding out about the Halloween mask smell gave me the same uncanny eerie feeling as when I found out that the Boney M. singer isn't the black dancer but an older German guy, and the black dancer can’t really sing at all. Or when I heard the burglar's warning music in The Sims 1 for the first time ever in my life, exploding from my speakers.<br />
<br />
Opening note: 8<br />
Sillage/Projection: 7+<br />
Dry down: 9-<br />
Longevity: 9-<br />
Blend/Composition: 10<br />
Versatility: 6-<br />
Uniqueness: 8+<br />
Value for money: 7<br />
Bottle design/Aesthetics: 9<br />
Overall experience: 9-<br />
Blind-buy rating: 5-</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="19668"comment_id="2040045"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Rasasi/La-Yuqawam-Homme-19668.html?ccid=2040045#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2035273" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(247,244,242,0.76);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:1,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc1990088" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="𝕪𝕒𝕔𝕙𝕥𝕞𝕒𝕤𝕥𝕖𝕣"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1489951"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.1489951.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="𝕪𝕒𝕔𝕙𝕥𝕞𝕒𝕤𝕥𝕖𝕣" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma1990088ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck2x2"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd1990088" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(249,249,243,0.85); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1489951">𝕪𝕒𝕔𝕙𝕥𝕞𝕒𝕤𝕥𝕖𝕣</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2023-12-01">12/01/23 15:24</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>This is my first review on this site, and it's for a reason. I want to warn you.<br />
<br />
After a month of researching this perfume online, due to it not being available for testing anywhere, I blind-bought it. I heard all about how it's extremely masculine and an amazing performer.<br />
<br />
Let me summarize the 2023 batches: It's sweet-fruity with a hint of leather. Performance is average. Nothing to be excited about, and comparing it to a legend like Tom Ford Tuscan Leather is a little bit insulting.<br />
<br />
Presentation: The wooden box is gone, and you get a cardboard box with a wood color. Not a bad presentation, but clearly a downgrade.<br />
Bottle: The magnetic cap is gone, and you get just a regular cap. The atomizer is good. <br />
Scent: Can't speak about the older batches, but at the moment, this perfume is 100% unisex because of the sweetness that greatly overpowers the best part of the scent - the leather notes, which are amazing. For me, it's the exact leather note from Tom Ford Ombre Leather. Great scent, it's just too feminine for a "masculine" leather fragrance.<br />
Performance: Average, 6 hours at best. Clearly a surprise after the thousand reviews of older batches which stated 16 hours and more.<br />
<br />
I bought it for 70€. I was choosing between this and Gucci Intense Oud, which was 90€. Obvious mistake on my part, but it's kind of different, and I'm happy to have it in my collection.<br />
<br />
If you want a great leather fragrance, get Tom Ford Ombre Leather when it's on sale.<br />
<br />
3/5 - Rasasi messed up this fragrance in every way possible for more profit.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="19668"comment_id="1990088"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Rasasi/La-Yuqawam-Homme-19668.html?ccid=1990088#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent1983985" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(254,252,238,0.72);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:0,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1478553">suzanne_ronald</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2023-09-07">09/07/23 07:00</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>If there was such a thing as BLACK FOREST LEATHER....  In the first couple of minutes I can feel the raspberry and already the leather-oud is swelling through.  As the sillage opens up the raspberry gets juicier and punctuated with saffron and faint thyme.  Transitioning to the heart, the raspberry-leather deepens, taking on some smoky, musky &amp; animalic notes.  This all rests on a leather-suede base built from oud-ambroxan with some amber-woody touches.  This is a dupe of Tuscan Leather Tom Ford with good approximation and excellent performance.  It's targeted to men but I find it unisex, although last year I gave this in a group of fragrances to my nephew and he ended up giving it back because he thought it was too feminine with the raspberry.  I was so happy to get it back because the raspberry has gotten more intense as the bottle has aged, but after the first hour it's softer and the  leather-y oud-incense notes come on strong.   As a kid I had a dark leather pair of shoes that my uncle called "ox-blood leather", but in my imagination for naming leathers, this is like the black forest cake of leather (although there's leather instead of chocolate, it's there in my imagination).   It's a total love for me.  10/10.  Enjoy!</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="19668"comment_id="1921910"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Rasasi/La-Yuqawam-Homme-19668.html?ccid=1921910#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent1920380" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,245,242,0.77);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:3,&quot;winter&quot;:1,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:3,&quot;sillage&quot;:2,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;unisex&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;had&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="3"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; Ombre Leather), but for what it costs nor would you expect it to be. La Yuqawam Homme is horribly synthetic and excessively sweet to my nose. I’m assuming that’s the artificial raspberry, but I don’t get the fruitiness on my skin. I also get an off-putting motor oil like note in this one. Performance from my September 2020 batch is nuclear, and it’s headache inducing. I notice it seems to get even stronger every year with age as well if you can believe that! I guess you have to give Rasasi credit for being true to their tagline “Make your presence felt”. A more suitable tagline might have been “Punch everyone in the room in the head”. Might try layering it with WD-40 or brake cleaner to tone it down a bit.<br />
<br />
Like the city it hails from, it’s a perfect literal metaphor of pure materialism without context, culture, or value. Tasteless, over the top, and gaudy.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="19668"comment_id="1743779"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Rasasi/La-Yuqawam-Homme-19668.html?ccid=1743779#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent1740394" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(254,252,238,0.8);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:3,&quot;winter&quot;:1,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="3"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1652418">L&#039;Eau Jeff</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2023-01-21">01/21/23 20:27</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>As a new collector, my first Rasasi purchase was Ambergris Showers; which I do like. <br />
I am very impressed with the presentation and love the magnetic capped wooden box. The bottle is great as well; it feels solid in the hand. <br />
My very next Rasasi was La Yaqawam Pour Homme. Based on my research I was expecting the same presentation as Amergris Showers. What arrived at my door was……disappointing. <br />
The box was now made of hard cardboard with no magnetic cap. Instead, the upper half slides snuggly over the inner gold band that separates the two halves.  <br />
I bought the bottle on Amazon for a normal price and “Intense Oud” out of Chicago fulfilled the order. <br />
The bottle itself and the fragrance are wonderful. The only difference that I can see between ambergris showers, tobacco blaze, and this bottle, the presentation box.<br />
When I reached out to Intense Oud asking if they knew anything about Rasasi cheapening the box to cut costs, or if perhaps, maybe they sold me a fake, they kept sending me the same cookie cutter “quality is our number one priority email…”<br />
I don’t know if this happens to anybody else because I’m new to this game, but checking the batch code seems next to impossible on this product. <br />
So I’m extremely curious… Has anybody had any similar experience to this with this fragrance? Again the perfume itself is fantastic. It’s one of my favorites.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="19668"comment_id="1740211"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Rasasi/La-Yuqawam-Homme-19668.html?ccid=1740211#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent1739317" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,245,242,0.73);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:1,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:4,&quot;sillage&quot;:3,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;male&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; Obviously the TF Tuscan Leather is a superb quality fragrance. On the other hand, I won't brush off La Yuqawam Homme by Rasasi so quick. <br />
When I spray La Yuqawam Homme it on my skin, it smells 99% the same to TF. The sweetness of raspberry fades away, I find the leather/suede notes are more than decent..at least 8/10. <br />
This is one of those purfume that you shouldn't snub your nose at. Considering the price and how much time Rasasi put into producing a good quality juice. <br />
This juice is perfect for fall/winter months. I would be surprised if you wore it at a party, and someone came up to you and commented it's not TF?<br />
Longevity and Sillage is excellent at least 6hrs plus.<br />
The version I have is well over 6 year's old. I use my TF just as much. Sometimes I'll go to La Yuqawam Homme because I enjoy the aroma this juice it gives me. 8.5/10</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="19668"comment_id="1726487"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Rasasi/La-Yuqawam-Homme-19668.html?ccid=1726487#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent1724559" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(248,249,236,0.75);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:0,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:4,&quot;sillage&quot;:3,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;male&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1522368">Dnichl</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2022-12-20">12/20/22 15:03</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>First few times using it i could pick out the cocaine accord people are always taking about. but after that i really couldn't find it anymore. i guess my brain was still learning to process the different notes and put it all together.<br />
<br />
Performance off the bat was below expectation. about 4hrs on skin 6hrs on clothes. after using 100 sprays or so and letting the bottle macerate for a few months, performance has increased significantly. projects well for 3-4hrs hanging on til around 8hrs in and it falls off into a skin scent. 10+ on clothes. the raspberry opening was tamed and smoothed out in that time as well. fresh out of the box the raspberry was punchy and sharp. <br />
<br />
10/10 frag -fantastic clone. truly sets the bar for how good clones can get.<br />
9/10 value -much cheaper than TF but this is overpriced due to the hype. 10/10 if it was maybe ~$15 cheaper.<br />
<br />
edit: i just looked at the prices and it's even worse than i thought. it used to be ~$40 before the hype, i bought it when it was around $65, now prices are $90-150. with discounters mostly sold out. this should AT MOST be a $80 clone frag.<br />
<br />
*Canadian dollars</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="19668"comment_id="1713685"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Rasasi/La-Yuqawam-Homme-19668.html?ccid=1713685#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent1712112" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(254,252,238,0.75);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:2,&quot;winter&quot;:1,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:3,&quot;sillage&quot;:2,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;unisex&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="2"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc1687899" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="Gidimeister"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/942126"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/himg/o.69247.png" class="comments-avatar"alt="Gidimeister" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"><span class="idLinkify" title="/perfume/Estee-Lauder/Lauder-for-Men-532.html"><img loading="lazy" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/perfume/mm.532.jpg"class="perfume-wearing-icon" alt="Lauder for Men"title="Lauder for Men"></span></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma1687899ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck3x1"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd1687899" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(250,247,236,0.83); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/942126">Gidimeister</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2022-11-13">11/13/22 23:07</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>I generally enjoy leathers, but as I live in a Mediterranean climate, I need airy leathers like Dior’s Farenheit, Tom Ford’s Ombre Leather, Aramis by Aramis, Chanel’s Antaeus and so on, the ones that allow other notes to sparkle and live alongside it. <br />
<br />
This is nothing like those. La Yuqawam wears heavy, absolutely pulverising the senses throughout its fragrance journey. The first spray smells a bit like being doused in kerosene. You hear a lot of talk in the community about Dior’s Farenheit having a vague petrol smell, but I have never gotten that. This, on the other hand, smells something like a fuel depot in a third world country. <br />
<br />
You have to wait a few hours to get something reasonably smooth and enjoyable. This is the middle of the fragrance journey, when all the notes are in balance. The raspberry comes out and blends wonderfully with spices and a bitter leather that reminds me of a punchier Ombre Leather. I like this part. I caught myself thinking that this might smell a bit like the birch beast Club De Nuit Intense Man. This part lingers the longest, thankfully. <br />
<br />
But by its final stages, 12+ hours later, the tar returns and you get something that smells a bit like the butt of a used cigarette clinging to your clothes.<br />
<br />
As I said, I love me a good leather, but this is simply not for me. It is far too much perfume for my nose, even with just two shy sprays.<br />
<br />
Ps: Airiness is my preference. Some like dense fragrances that practically commandeer the entire surroundings wherever they go. I cannot stand that. So read my comments with that in mind. If you like heavy fragrances and/or live in a temperate country with long cold seasons then this might be up your alley.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="19668"comment_id="1687899"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Rasasi/La-Yuqawam-Homme-19668.html?ccid=1687899#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent1679849" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,249,251,0.77);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:4,&quot;sillage&quot;:3,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1414376">m373x</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2022-10-23">10/23/22 04:34</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>Sweet masculine raspberry leather petrol opening. Dark and warm. Very pleasant. Bold but wearable. Bad boy vibes all day. Gradually loses sweetness and the fruitiness of the raspberry as it dries down. Late dry down is mainly  smoky leather and not as interesting and nuanced as the first few hours but still really good. The leather in this is excellently done and the main player throughout. <br />
<br />
BATCH# R3022154/F1075761  ; Manufacturing date: April 2021 ; <br />
<br />
Initially this had the same great scent profile but very bad performance: 3-4 hours longevity. 3 months later the longevity has practically doubled with improved projection too. Now 1 year later this has macerated beastly: 14+ hours longevity with 4-5 hours of moderate projection before withdrawing closer to the skin. If your bottle has bad performance initially don't be discouraged, it will improve. I spray this 3-5 times.<br />
<br />
Day and night wear, masculine. Suitable for cold and warm but maybe not for hot weather. Easy to wear photorealistic leather but not for the office.<br />
<br />
10/10</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="19668"comment_id="1672272"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Rasasi/La-Yuqawam-Homme-19668.html?ccid=1672272#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent1668056" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,249,251,0.79);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:1,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:5,&quot;sillage&quot;:3,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;male&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; Next!</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="19668"comment_id="1659037"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Rasasi/La-Yuqawam-Homme-19668.html?ccid=1659037#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent1658579" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,249,251,0.8);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:1,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:4,&quot;sillage&quot;:3,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;male&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1239768">Ryanne4707</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2022-09-19">09/19/22 15:58</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>Definitely a divisive fragrance. You will either like it or hate it. My initial reaction was dirty suede. Overwhelming dirty suede. Not new car leather, but what a shoe cobblers shop that only makes suede shoes would smell like. So the guy below, who says he doesn't get leather, you need to reverse your nose job. There is a sweetness that sits behind the suede that hints at raspberry, but it's not overwhelming or very distinguishable. But it's a nice touch that is definitely necessary for this fragrance to work. Super dry and long lasting. A little goes a long way.  Definitely gentlemanly and sophisticated. Good for date night and formal events in fall or winter weather. I wouldn't wear this to the office as it's not going to be well received by everyone. The scent bubble that trails you is a lot more palatable, and I guess that's the point. leans Uber masculine but not every man will be able to pull this off. I picture George Clooney, or Javier barden wearing this. So if your 5 ft 2 this might not be for you.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="19668"comment_id="1648571"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Rasasi/La-Yuqawam-Homme-19668.html?ccid=1648571#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent1640873" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(247,244,242,0.76);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:4,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:3,&quot;sillage&quot;:2,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;unisex&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="4"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1026158">bintTapputi</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2022-09-08">09/08/22 09:05</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>Recently compared this with Tom Ford's Ombre Leather so I'll share my thoughts. First, I don't think there is a remarkable similarity in the two perfumes, for the majority of their stay. There are some waxing and waning periods where I can see why the two are compared, but overall they are ultimately different beasts. La Yuqawam لا يقاوم meaning something that doesn't resist, aka irresistible. First impressions, dry vetiver + Lattafa woodiness. This is an outdoorsy, dirty fragrance, extremely warm and bright. I don't really get a leather impression, at least not leather like in a car or a purse. Rather maybe leather as in the skin of an animal? Overall it's just not my impression, this is a rather woody fragrance for me/there is a pencil-shaving note of some kind. It's very dry. Projection wise, and how long it lasts, it's good. It's not Ombre Leather "good" but I actually prefer the moderation here. 3 liberal sprays gave enough projection to last several hours and enjoy the dry down. There is also some weird fruitiness that comes through here and there, like the peel of fruit or the rind. I say that specifically cause it's not juicy, but it is a dry sweetness. Definitely think this is unisex, I think it makes for a great base in layering perfumes. I think it will work with almost any fem fragrance because it's dirtiness isn't animalic, rather, actually dirty like the earth. Either way, it's really rather enjoyable and I'll adore my 5ml sample for as long as I can. 8/10</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="19668"comment_id="1640873"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Rasasi/La-Yuqawam-Homme-19668.html?ccid=1640873#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent1635944" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(248,249,236,0.85);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:0,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; I think it's the raspberry that throws it off for me. I got this before I tried TF TL, so I thought I'd get a decant of TL to see if I liked it better. I do not. Same goes for PDM Godolphin. I would like a good clone of Ombre Leather because that is my favorite leather fragrance. If anyone has any suggestions, I would appreciate it.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="19668"comment_id="1635944"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Rasasi/La-Yuqawam-Homme-19668.html?ccid=1635944#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent1631557" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(254,252,238,0.86);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:1,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:4,&quot;sillage&quot;:3,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;male&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; My batch is 2022 and the longevity and sillage is beastly. I can't get enough of this. Projection is easily 8-12h. Starts with very fruity scent and settles down to very pleasant sweet leathery scent which last without any nuances.<br />
<br />
This is one of a few fragrances which I can't stop smelling out of my body. It is really addictive. I don't have any feedback from the female side regarding this fragrance, but in general ladies usually are not such a big fans of leather fragrances as men in my surroundings.<br />
<br />
I got my Ombré Leather and immediately fall in love with leather fragrances. So I was very curious about this one. If I compare them side by side, they are very similar, but I like La Yuqawam even more for it fruity scent. Ombre Leather on the other side smell for me more luxurious. But the difference is negligible. They are both great fragrances.<br />
<br />
This is my signature fragrance until I find some other to beat this beast. 4.8/5</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="19668"comment_id="1631557"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Rasasi/La-Yuqawam-Homme-19668.html?ccid=1631557#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent1630921" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(248,249,236,0.76);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:1,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:4,&quot;sillage&quot;:3,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;male&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;had&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; <br />

<br />

This is my signature scent in the fall/winter. This fragrance smells very high quality for the price!<br />

Lol For me awsome very happy with the purchase!</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="19668"comment_id="1513468"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Rasasi/La-Yuqawam-Homme-19668.html?ccid=1513468#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent1513052" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(248,249,236,0.88);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:1,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:4,&quot;sillage&quot;:2,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;male_unisex&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc1513052" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="perfidious_script"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1348389"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.1348389.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="perfidious_script" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma1513052ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck0x3"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd1513052" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(248,249,236,0.88); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1348389">perfidious_script</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2022-02-27">02/27/22 09:05</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>Blind buy. Found this (like many others) after trying TFTL and doing a little research.<br />
<br />
The first spray seemed true to the common promise: 'a TFTL clone at a fraction of the price'. Intense, dry, medicinal/chemical leather with little else going on. I loved it. When my partner came into our (fairly small) place a few hours later she noticed it immediately, and was a little worried.<br />
<br />
In the following days (and following sprays) the other notes started to come come through: the sweet fruity notes, a light woody accord, that deep animalic/woody pencil-shaving note and other subtle accords that are a bit more tricky to identify.<br />
<br />
Calling this 'just a TFTL clone' seems unfair and a little short sighted to me. Certainly the base notes are close enough to be nearly indistinguishable, but La-Yuqawum is more rounded, and softer IMO. Plus it seems to stick around longer. Too, looking down on this is a mere dupe seems unwarranted. This is a high quality perfume that takes the idea of a rough and medicinal leather perfume and puts a spin on it. After all we talk about 'Chypre' and 'Fougere' perfumes as classes, so why not 'Tuscan Leathers'?</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="19668"comment_id="1513052"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Rasasi/La-Yuqawam-Homme-19668.html?ccid=1513052#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent1510239" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(254,252,238,0.85);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:1,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:5,&quot;sillage&quot;:3,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;male&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; Leather, suede and sweet raspberry. After an hour I start to get hints of the jasmine, saffron and amber. The amber mellows it out a little, but not a heap. This is a leather beast. A very sweet beast with the raspberry. <br />
<br />
Very much Tuscan Leather, except TF initial application is much smoother. First 10 mins and somebody has thrown me in the petrol tank. <br />
<br />
Winter or Autumn nights out. Denim or leather jacket, white shirt, jeans and white shoes, or boots. <br />
<br />
It’s a strong vibe but a good vibe. Not an everyday or casual everyday type of scent though so this bottle will last. <br />
<br />
Opening 2/10 (douse yourself in petrol)<br />
Projection 8/10<br />
Longevity 10/10<br />
Price 8/10.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="19668"comment_id="1510239"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Rasasi/La-Yuqawam-Homme-19668.html?ccid=1510239#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent1505644" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(255,253,234,0.77);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/796916">Louismanuel</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2022-01-24">01/24/22 03:53</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>For me too much Tuscan Leather Clone. Not the kind of leather that I like most. But if that is what you are looking for, it may be a much affordable alternative. I own a 30 ML Tuscan Leather for which I paid around 90 €. <br />
I prefer Goldolphin, Aqua di Parma Leather or Ombre Leather. But are more expensive. <br />
If it is an in the face kind of leather you're looking for, you should go for the original Classic leather Knize Ten.<br />
Finally I believe Shay &amp; Blue London, Blacks Club Leather maybe a very good. more civilized alternative. I had a very good deal for it: 89 €/100 ML.<br />
All these have a very good performance.<br />
But for me, nothing beats the PdM Golden Bottle.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="19668"comment_id="1489710"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Rasasi/La-Yuqawam-Homme-19668.html?ccid=1489710#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent1488554" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,247,236,0.89);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:1,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:5,&quot;sillage&quot;:3,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;male&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1414461">THE BLESSED</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2022-01-05">01/05/22 17:37</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>I don't know about the reformulation issues for this one, but at the beginning I was happy to wear it, but after a while I lose my excitement to wear it, I was confused, nothing leathery, just synthetic fruity note in the dray down, I found the scent smillar to Arabian hooka or Shisha tobacco (hubbly bubbly) nothing wow, I found it not that friendly or versatile, anyway there are so many choices worth the try more than this.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="19668"comment_id="1477061"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Rasasi/La-Yuqawam-Homme-19668.html?ccid=1477061#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent1474005" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(254,252,238,0.85);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:4,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="4"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc1474005" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="jasontallwood"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1111570"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/himg/o.69247.png" class="comments-avatar"alt="jasontallwood" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma1474005ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck1x2"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd1474005" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(254,252,238,0.85); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1111570">jasontallwood</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2021-12-31">12/31/21 14:32</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>The batch code is at the bottom of the wooden box. It is not on the bottle. Under the cap or anything else. I actually checked when someone asked. Usually I don't care for batch codes but figure I'll help you guys out. <br />
<br />
I've never smelled Tuscan Leather or Ombre Leather this is often compared to but on a first impression it's slightly above average. I honestly didn't get it. I liked it but not 10/10 get 5 backup bottles now! However after wearing this for almost 2 years where the fragrance aged. The projection and longevity have greatly improved. You get this burst of freshly picked rasberries that splash you in the nose, then it transitions into a smooth leather that to some can come off as abrasive but I think it's really well done for a fragrance this masculine and there's some smoke in the background to give this definition. I absolutely see why someone would say this smells like being in the back of a luxury car smoking a cigar as every time you sniff your shirt or my case back of  my hand right now it's like I'm taking a drag on a cigarette. i've heard there are subtle differences with the real Tuscan leather but considering the price difference I couldn't care less The sweetness makes this fragrance almost addictive, where you look forward to wearing the fragrance again and again. <br />
<br />
As this dries down there's a bit of a middle eastern touch to this. Possibly how the thyme spice is used but you've really got to over think it to pick it up. So far the 10 or so people I've shown this fragrance to everyone seemed to enjoy it. One friend more than likely bought a bottle. Two cheap skate family members couldn't justify the price tag. Even when I told them how much the real tuscan leather is. <br />
<br />
Projection and longevity. Give it a few weeks and it drastically improves. I've had this happen quite a lot with certain EDP concentrated fragrances the first few years, I got well over 8 to 10 hours with this. The last time I wore this on the bus I did 5 sprays. I'm sure that's why this kid moved the second there was another empty seat on the bus beside me. <br />
<br />
Any time it gets cold out I'd put this on. As there's something perfectly fitting for the winter about this as there's some warmth and spiciness that comes from this fragrance. I can see myself wearing this as a first fragrance, it will excel in a suit, especially if you're a boss or manager. Fancy dinners and maybe date night. Though I can't see people clubbing in this, cuddling with someone or wearing this in the day time or to the gym. <br />
<br />
You'll like this if you're a fan of darker fragrances. Armani Code (EDT) immediately comes to mind. You've got to love leather. It has this nice sweetness to make it wearable more than a few times a year like a garbage niche fragrance no ones going to buy. The big difference is this goes in a whole different direction than code. Code is dark and sweet. This is richer due to more leather being used. Spicier and more aggressive. There will be times code works better, there will be times la yuqawam works better. <br />
<br />
I wish they would have released this without the stupid wooden box and the fancy bottle. I'd seriously be happy with glass bottles with the names on them. No one is going to see the bottles and I'd own tobacco blaze and ambergris showers already if they weren't almost $80 each because of the stupid presentation.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1402851">jbeck97</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2021-12-25">12/25/21 10:59</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>Such a great fragrance. I absolutely love TF Tuscan Leather, but I don't love the price.  This is an amazing clone that seems to perform just as well as TL on my skin, and it also projects very well while being affordable.  I find the leather note to be ever so slightly different from TF, but not so much that it makes a difference. It may be a little sharper, I can't quite put my finger on it, but whatever the difference it's so subtle that you can't really tell unless you compare the two side by side (which is what I did). <br />
When you're reading the reviews about it being watered down or not having much performance, just remember that this is only how it is perceived by those individuals, and as far as performance goes it can vary from person to person. These things are very subjective; I suggest you get your own nose on it and see how it reacts to your specific skin and chemistry before making a decision.  <br />
It's an awesome raspberry leather fragrance, and if you like tuscan leather but don't like dropping that much money on a bottle, you should definitely try this one out.  Don't let the negative comments stop you from trying this one, most of those people are full of shit anyways.  :)</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="19668"comment_id="1470103"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Rasasi/La-Yuqawam-Homme-19668.html?ccid=1470103#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent1466064" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(254,252,238,0.82);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:0,&quot;winter&quot;:1,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:4,&quot;sillage&quot;:3,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;male&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc1448935" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="flekter"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1416655"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/himg/o.69247.png" class="comments-avatar"alt="flekter" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma1448935ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck4x2"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd1448935" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(250,245,242,0.89); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1416655">flekter</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2021-11-19">11/19/21 17:07</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>This is my first ever review on Fragrantica so I will probably not be the most specialized reviewer but I will give you my honest take on La Yuqawam. <br />
<br />
First of all, the perfume opens with a sweet raspberry note and the leather is instantly present. As time passes, it evolves into a beautiful mixture of these two notes. I do get the smokiness from it and I have to say I really love it. I am very sensitive to sweet aromas so this one is really cloying in the beginning but then tones down to a gorgeous masculine leather scent with a playful, fruity twist. <br />
<br />
As far as performance goes, I wore this 6 hours ago and as I am sitting on my bed after a club night, I can still absolutelt smell this one on me. I was catching whifs of it all night even in an environment where you normally have tons of perfume around you. I feel like anyone in a radius of 1 meter or more could smell it. <br />
<br />
I have a 2021 batch so I can’t speak for the older ones, but this thing has incredible performance for it’s price. It’s genuinely such a refined (although it might seem linear to some) fragrance that comes at a surprising price. However, this might not be for anyone. Sweet perfumes give me headaches and the intense raspberry of this gave me a slight headache as well. Yet I still wore it again because at the drydown, it doesnt’t bother me anyone.<br />
<br />
Great scent, great price, hard to recommend for a blind buy. Give samples a shot and see how it reacts on your skin. <br />
<br />
9/10 for me personally<br />
<br />
Update: It’s been nearly 24 hours since I wore the scent. Two showers after and numerous hand washes and hand sanitizers, I can still smell the perfume on my wrists where I rubbed it in. Performance is insane. Not sure what others are getting but if this is not beast performance I don’t know what is.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="19668"comment_id="1448935"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Rasasi/La-Yuqawam-Homme-19668.html?ccid=1448935#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent1443365" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(249,249,243,0.86);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:1,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:5,&quot;sillage&quot;:3,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;male&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/48578">fanzypants</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2021-10-24">10/24/21 10:05</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>Fall in Toronto, about 10 degrees over freezing.  Just traded for this and it's awesome!  Up there with my favourites.  <br />
<br />
While I generally get overwhelmed by middle eastern produced / branded fragrances with incense and or amber related components, this one works for me. <br />
Starting out with berry, it balances well against the leather.  As it dries, the florals really make this interesting and romantic while the incense and wood blend bring some roughness to it, a little ashy feel.  Love it!  I think the herbs and amber must help everything come together.   Wicked fall scent. <br />
In my collection, I also have sterling's just jack Italian leather which is awesome.  In comparison, this lasts longer and has more layers and development before settling on something much smoother.  Paying twice the price for this is worth it if you like wearing this scent in cooler weather.   It's going to get a lot of play for me.  <br />
Big thank you to the fragrantica user who traded this to me, and to all who left honest reviews!</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="19668"comment_id="1433796"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Rasasi/La-Yuqawam-Homme-19668.html?ccid=1433796#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent1427937" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,249,251,0.76);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:1,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:5,&quot;sillage&quot;:4,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;male&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; If you like TL I'm almost certain you'll like this.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="19668"comment_id="1418191"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Rasasi/La-Yuqawam-Homme-19668.html?ccid=1418191#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent1418131" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(255,253,234,0.83);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:0,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; Ive adpoted it as my signature scent because I really enjoy getting whiffs all day anyday anytime any occasion, however its best suited for colder evenings. 10/10 dont blind buy</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="19668"comment_id="1411706"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Rasasi/La-Yuqawam-Homme-19668.html?ccid=1411706#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent1410516" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,245,242,0.72);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:1,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:4,&quot;sillage&quot;:3,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;male&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; I like them both in a different way.  I tested it side by side on my left and right wrists and here is what my nose reported to me. I can easily tell the original even if it was a blind test. If you smell the original, you know what I'm talking about. Yes, there is a similarity in the scent profile. It's close but not very close. However, this doesn't mean that La Yuqawam is not good. It actually is, in its own right. To me, nothing beats the original period. The OG has a sharper, distinct opening but this one has a softer opening and as it evolves, I find it more wearable and has a much pleasant fruity dry down. I have to have this in my collection and I want to wear this as well. As to the original, I'll wear that on more special occasion or events.<br />
<br />
If you like the original, it wouldn't hurt to check this out as an addition to your collection. At that price point, I would say this is a bang for your buck. <br />
<br />
I'll rate this humble but wonderful juice a 9.5/10<br />

The differences are slightly noticeable but as scents vary depending on skin chemistry i'd be shocked to find someone who will smell this on a person and not think it was Tuscan Leather.  I did a side by side and the differences are so slight it amazed me. Another Middle Eastern Frag with quality ingredients making a Niche scent from a western brand seem unnecessary. <br />
<br />
This scent lasts on my skin at least 9 hours and on my clothes double that plus. The sillage was strong for the first 3 hours before settling down to a still very noticeable scent cloud for another 3 hours. After this it became more close to the skin but hardly dead. I smelled it on myself without trying 9 hours into 5 initial sprays.<br />
<br />
LY has a very nice raspberry note which lasts longer than the same note in TL. This makes LY more wearable as a result. I receive a TON on compliments when i wear this out. I've heard this a few time also..."Tuscan Leather, Right?"...I just laugh in my head and say in response, "Nice Guess"...lmao...A women in a bar actually said I smelled like Cocaine...I've heard people, including the rapper Drake, make that same comment about TL. Go figure...La Yuqawam is one of the best alternatives to a niche scent ever made under $75.  If TL and LY were both made by Creed, TL would be Batch# blah blah and La Yuqawam would be Batch# blah blah blah. <br />
<br />
9/10<br />
<br />
YouTube Channel- Simply Put Scents</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="19668"comment_id="623930"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Rasasi/La-Yuqawam-Homme-19668.html?ccid=623930#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent676341" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(255,253,234,0.71);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:1,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:5,&quot;sillage&quot;:3,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; These fragrances could easily be confused by your average person, and imo LY to be could easily compete with TL. I find this has more dimension, complexity and the notes are a better balance, leading to a smoother product. I adore TL, but it is much heavier on the leather, which almost gives it a chemical, synthetic feel at first. You don't have to search for the other notes in La Yuqawam, like you do in TL. In LY the juicy raspberries, sultry saffron, masculine woods all have a strong presence to seduce the strong leather, suede into balanced perfection. This starts out as a fresh burst of rich red raspberries and smokey leather. As this dries down, the woods and saffron become more noticeable, but the leather, suede and raspberry still remain present and strong. <br />
<br />
For me this was a blind buy, and it paid off. I no longer have any desire to get a full-size bottle of TL. If you like TL, but want a smoother, more rounded fragrance and don't want to fall behind on rent, then go for LY. <br />
<br />
This comes in a beautiful wooden box with copper-colored metallic accents. The bottle itself is a thick, rich Amber glass with an engraved wooden cap. The whole presentation is luxurious and extravagant like the city where it comes from, Dubai.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="19668"comment_id="676341"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Rasasi/La-Yuqawam-Homme-19668.html?ccid=676341#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2272250" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(254,252,238,0.84);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:1,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:4,&quot;sillage&quot;:3,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;male_unisex&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;want&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%;
