This used to be one of the strongest scent but they have reformulated the product. A bait and switch.<br />
<br />
Old strong scent came in a firm wooden box. My bottle was manufactured in 2023, and it now it comes in a cheap cardboard box. That's fine but the worst part is that it has been reformulated. What once used to perform for 10-12 hours is now a 1 hour fragrance. <br />
<br />
Scent is literally gone in an hour, and this is after a fresh shower. I've never been so mad with a company.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="19668"comment_id="1902788"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Rasasi/La-Yuqawam-Homme-19668.html?ccid=1902788#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent1441451" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,249,251,0.75);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:1,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:1,&quot;sillage&quot;:1,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;male&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="1"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1407107">Khatrissimusdorsi</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2021-11-06">11/06/21 18:01</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>Recently purchased a La Yuqawam Pour Homme from Dubai, in Rasasi's official store. It was out of stock in practically all their stores except for one which had stock that I could find.<br />
<br />
<br />
The performance is absolutely horrid. Let alone myself, even the people who are sat 5 inches away from me can't smell the scent 15 minutes after I've applied it. I asked my cousin who was sat next to me whether he could smell anything (and he usually smells and comments on whatever fragrance I've put on without me even asking), and he said no. Then he sniffed my skin/clothes and said yeah, but this scent is super light.<br />
<br />
I'd sprayed 6-7 sprays, on clothes and skin, just about 25 minutes before this moment.<br />
<br />
<br />
Paid about $75 for this scent and expected a hell of a lot more, especially considering this price was not easy for me to pay. <br />
<br />
<br />
People used to speak very highly of this fragrance, but I'm not sure Rasasi have maintained their quality. <br />
<br />
<br />
.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="19668"comment_id="1441451"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Rasasi/La-Yuqawam-Homme-19668.html?ccid=1441451#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent1174496" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,245,242,0.82);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:2,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="2"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%;
